[2023-03-07, 18:14:02] Deelaka Dias: Writing is a high beneficial activity which helps to improve our grammar, sharp writing creativity and expressing our own ideas in a pleasant manner etc. All these can be done if we can write our day today incidents in book which is called diary or without keeping them privately we can share them all over the world using blog writing.

I like to share the things I faced on days only with my family members and friends who I really trust. Because I have faced to many incidents which made me really uncomfortable in a large crowd during my school life. That does not meant that I wrote blogs during my school, but I shared my some experiences which made me trouble just to avoid my friends facing them. But final result was they use those to tease me. So I decided not to share them anymore with anyone. We must be intelligent to understand that each and everyone had to face to this cruel situation when writing blogs. Writing a blogs can help people in many ways. Since you share your own pure experiences with them. For an example if you are writing blogs on your daily routine, people definitely find thousand of advices to their lives. 

Keeping a diary to maintain your personal experiences is much safer according to my own perspective. And you do not need to use electronic equipments to write your routine, so you are free of any disease which may caused by those devices. On the other hand when you are a blog writer, you need to remain considerable amount of your valuable time to write them creatively, have to make sure no grammatical errors in your content and it is harmless to anyone, if not next you may have to face to huge trouble. But when you writing them privately, do not need to consider about any of those factors.

[2023-04-22, 22:26:06] Deelaka Dias: Sure, let me explain this in more detail.

The median of a set of data is the value that lies in the middle of the dataset when the values are arranged in ascending or descending order. For example, if we have a set of 5 numbers {2, 4, 5, 7, 9}, the median is 5 because it is the middle number when the values are arranged in ascending order.

However, in a normal distribution, the data is symmetric around the mean. This means that the same number of data points lie on either side of the mean. Therefore, the median is also the same as the mean for a normal distribution.

So, if we have a normal distribution with a mean of 47, then the median is also approximately 47. This is because the distribution is symmetric around the mean, so the value in the middle of the dataset is also the same as the mean.

Therefore, we can say that the median mark in the class is approximately 47.
